target=\"_blank\">Give</a></li>\t\t</ul>\n\t</nav>\n</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</header>\n\n\t<main id=\"main\" name=\"main\" tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"page main faculty-profile\">\n\t\t<a class=\"show-on-focus\" href=\"#js-global-footer\" tabindex=\"0\">Jump to Footer</a>\n\n\t\t<section class=\"faculty-masthead\">\n\n\t\t\t<figure>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"image\" style=\"background-image: url('https://engineering.virginia.edu/sites/default/files/biocomp-masthead.jpg')\" role=\"img\"></div>\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"caption-wrapper\">\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"alignment\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"headshot\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<img src=\"https://engineering.virginia.edu/sites/default/files/styles/faculty_headshot/public/MadhavMarathecropped.jpeg?itok=_zyg6MvX\" alt=\"marathe image\">\t\t\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<h1>Madhav Marathe</h1>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"title\">Professor, Computer Science<br>Distinguished Professor in Biocomplexity, Biocomplexity Institute<br>Division Director, Network Systems Science and Advanced Computing Division, Biocomplexity Institute </span>\n\t\t\t\t\t</span>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"overlay\"></div>\n\n\t\t\t</figure>\n\n\t\t</section>\n\n\t\t<!-- breadcrumbs -->\n\t\t\t\t<nav class=\"breadcrumbs\">\n\t\t\t<ul>\n\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/\" class=\"home-link\"><span class=\"show-for-sr\">Home</span><svg class=\"icon icon-home\"><use xlink:href=\"#icon-home\"></use></svg></a>\n\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/faculty\">Find Faculty</a>\n\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"current\">Madhav Marathe</span>\n\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t</nav>\n\n\t\t<div class=\"wrapper row\">\n\n\t\t\t<section class=\"main-content column midway-8 midway-push-4 large-9 large-push-3\">\n\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<!-- page title and intro -->\n\t\t\t\t        \n<article class=\"user-markup native\">\n\n\t<h2 class=\"h1\">Bio</h2>\n\n\t\t<span class=\"credentials\">\n\t\t<span class=\"school\">BTech. Computer Science and Engineering, IIT Chennai, 1989</span><span class=\"school\">Ph.D. Computer Science, University at Albany-SUNY, 1994</span>\n\t</span>\n\t\n\t\n\t\t<blockquote class=\"quote\">\n\n\t\t\t<svg class=\"icon icon-shape\"><use xlink:href=\"#icon-shape\"></use></svg>\n\t\t\t\n\t\t\t<div class=\"wrap\">\n\n\t\t\t\t<p>\"Our research focus is to understand general principles that govern the design, analysis, control, and optimization of complex networks. We take a team science approach and develop innovative solutions  that have societal impact. \"</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t</blockquote>\n\n\t\n\t<!-- Content here -->\n\t<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h4>Research interests include:</h4>\n<p>\nNetwork Science, Machine Learning and Artificial Intelligence</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<p>Madhav Marathe is an endowed Distinguished Professor in&nbsp;Biocomplexity, Director of the Network Systems Science and Advanced Computing (NSSAC) Division, Biocomplexity Institute and Initiative, and a tenured Professor of Computer Science at the University of&nbsp;Virginia. Dr. Marathe is a passionate advocate and practitioner of transdisciplinary team science. During his 25-year professional career, he has established and led a number of large transdisciplinary projects and groups. His areas of expertise are network science, artificial intelligence, high performance computing, computational epidemiology, biological and socially coupled systems, and data analytics.</p>\n<p>From January 2005 to September 2018, he was a Professor of Computer Science at Virginia Tech. Concurrently, at Virginia Tech, he was&nbsp;the Deputy Director (2005-2014) and then the Director (2014-2018) of the Network Dynamics and Simulation Science Laboratory at the Biocomplexity Institute of Virginia Tech. He obtained his Bachelor of Technology degree in 1989 in Computer Science and Engineering from the Indian Institute of Technology, Madras, and his Ph.D. in 1994 in Computer Science from the University at Albany -SUNY, under the supervision of Professors Harry B. Hunt III and Richard E. Stearns. Before coming to Virginia Tech in 2005, he worked in the Basic and Applied Simulation Science group (CCS-5) in the Computer and Computational Sciences Division at Los Alamos National Laboratory where he was team leader in a theory-based, advanced simulation program to represent, design, and analyze extremely large socio-technical and critical infrastructure systems.&nbsp;He holds adjunct appointments at Chalmers University and the Indian Institute of Public Health.</p>\n<p>Dr. Marathe has published more than 350 articles in peer reviewed journals, conferences, and workshops. Mentoring and training next generation scientists has been his life-long passion. He has mentored more than a dozen staff scientists, and (co)-advised more than 20 doctoral students, 20+ MS students&nbsp;and 10+ postdoctoral fellows.</p>\n<p>Dr. Marathe and his division focus on developing the scientific foundations and the associated engineering principles to study large-scale biological, information, social, and technical (BIST) systems. His current interests span five broad themes: (<em>i</em>) methods to construct various BIST networks using partial and noisy data as well as procedural information; (<em>ii</em>) understanding the general form and structure of dynamical processes over BIST networks (e.g., key network/pathway properties and typical pathways that impact dynamics); (<em>iii</em>) algorithmic theory of optimization and control as it pertains to the dynamical processes, including methods to detect, enhance, arrest, and mitigate dynamics; (<em>iv</em>) general conceptual and algorithmic foundations to understand the co-evolution of networks and dynamics; and (<em>v</em>) high-performance services-based computing solutions that can be delivered seamlessly to end users and policy makers.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n</article>\n\n<div class=\"row\">\n\n\t\n\t\t<div class=\"columns large-6\">\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"faculty-info-section\">\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"user-markup heading\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"flag\"><svg class=\"icon icon-ribbon\"><use xlink:href=\"#icon-ribbon\"></use></svg></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<h2>Awards</h2>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t<ul algorithms and software systems for network science and public health epidemiology</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"item-sub\">2018</span>\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span System</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"item-sub\">2000</span>\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\n\t\n\t\n\t\t<div class=\"columns large-6\">\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"faculty-info-section\">\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"user-markup heading\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"flag\"><svg class=\"icon icon-research\"><use xlink:href=\"#icon-research\"></use></svg></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t<h2>Research Interests</h2>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t<ul class=\"items\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"item-title\">Network science</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"item-title\">Machine learning and artificial intelligence</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"item-title\">Discrete graphical dynamical systems and multi-agent systems</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"item-title\">Computational epidemiology, computational economics, computational immunology, and computational
